henotenkanha,shomotunojuyouwohukureagarasemasita.korenitaisishositatihamazu,teutusitoiugijutunowakunonakade,seisanseiwoagerutamenokuhuuwotumikasaneteikimasu.honbunnnoshushanisennnensurukoubougaarunakade,inisharuyashugakinitokkasitatokorogaumare,monnyouyasoushokuganihamata,betunokoubougasenmonnniatarutoittabungyoukagasusundeikimasita.nazorubekigennponwonanibunsatukaniwake,heikousitekakiutusinosagyouwosusumeruhousikigakakuritusaremasu.bungyouniyorukouritukanikuwae,koreniyottegennponwokakuteidekiruyouninattakotoha,dengonge-munokurikaesiniyorunoizunozoudaiwoosaeruuedemokoukagaarimasita.saraniitibuniha,genzainoka-bonnyousinisoutousuru,matuyaniworiyousitakopi-siwokuhuusite,seisanseiwoageyoutosurukokoromimoumaremasu.yo-roppaniokerutosiminshuunotaitouha,shomotunopeijiwomekuriagerukazedesita.kareraha,atarasiitisikiwokakutokusurutamenodouguyatanosiminotamenohonwomotome,shahonkoubounihasagyoukouritukanoaturyokugakakatteittanodesu.yo-roppaniokeruinsatujutuha,kousitesudeniryousannnoaturyokugatakamaritutuattasanakaniumaremasita.arakajimesonzaisiteitajuyounikotaeetakotode,konogijutuhakyuusokunihukyuusiteikimasu.katujiwomotiitainsatuha,gu-tenberukunisakanoborukotoyonhyakunenmae,kajiyaderenkinjutusidemoattatyuugokunohitunoboruniyottesudenikokoromirareteitatoiimasu.nendodeseikeisi,yaitekatakusitasuekatujiha,matuyaniyarou,kamibaiwonettetukuttasettyakuzaiwonuttateppannnoueninaraberare,tetuwakudekakomaretekoteisaremasita.korewokarukunessitekarasamasuto,itimainokappangadekimasu.insatugo,hanwonessinaoseba,katujiwobarabaranisitesairiyousurukotomokanoudesita.tyuuzoukatujinihanasiwokagittemo,tyousendehasudeni,ju-goseikizenhannnikonogijutugaumareteimasita.sumomoasasandaimenoou,taisouhasennyonhyakusannnenn,tyousennnishomotugasukunaikotowoureete,su-hyakumankonodoukatujinotyuuzouwosu-kagetudeikkyoniokonawasetatoiimasu.sonogomo,tudukuouniyotte,daikibonakatujinotyuuzougakurikaesaremasita.itarianiju-niseikinitutaerare,sonogoyo-roppakakutinihiromattakamiha,doubutunokawanitottekawaruankanahonnnosozai kuraihinimituketamonotu-rukittonitaisurukonohyoukakijiha,senkyu-hyakukyu-ju-sanheiseigotosinoitigatujuugonitinikakimasita.zenjitumadenimemowotorinagarasohutowotukattemite,genkouhakonohidekataduketeimasu.henshuushakararenrakuwomorattahiwotokuteisitari,genkouwokakumadenodandoriwosetumeidekirunoha,toujikanarikomakakunitijouwokirokusiteitakaradesu.senkyu-hyakukyu-ju-heiseinitosinonatukarakyuujuusannnennnoakinikaketaoyososannnennamarinoaida,watasihanikkiwokaiteimasita.huruibunshofairuwohipparidasiteyomikaesitatoki,konotu-rukittonohyoukakijinihaakaruityousiwokanjimasita.karukuotyaraketemoirusi,saigonotokoronado,imanimosikabannnoekisupandobukkuworyousansisounaikioidesu.keredohontounotokoro,toujinowatasihakanarisindoiseisinjoutainiarimasita.nikkiwotegakarini,toujinokokoronowadatiwotadotteikuto,konogenkounoakarusagamusiro,turakuomoetekimasu.mainitiwokirokusihajimetakikkakeha,byoukidesita.sanju-hassaininattemamonaku,watasihajibungayandeirukotowosirimasu.henshuupurodakushonwoyame,hitoridegenkouwokakihajimetekaranananenmeno,konotokimoharudesita.zassihenorensaiyatankoubonnnosippitunikuwae,toujihaterebinokouseinosigotonimotewosometeimasita.ippasinosigototyuudokunoyounakurasiwo,kokoronookudehasukositokuininattetuduketeitanodatoomoimasu.soregatotuzenn,namarinoyounayamainojihadagauitekite,karadagaugokanakunarimasita.kensakekkagadetebyoumeiwotugerutoki,saishonikakattajimotonobyouinnnoisigakomattayounakaowositeitanowooboeteimasu.onajibyoukinitukiatteitatijinnnotuyoisusumegaatte,senmonnnosekushonwomotubyouinwotazuneruto,suguninyuuinwosijisaremasita.natunohajimekarasankagetunyuuinsite,hantosigonoharunimouitido,byouinnnimodorukotoninarimasita.shokanitaiinsuruto,mamonakutitiganyuuinsimasu.kokyounohirosimanikaettetitinitukisoukotowokime,gimudukerareteirumainitinotentekiha,sonobyouindeiteruyoutehaisimasita.titigayuki,yokunennnoharunimatanyuuinn.gingahittihaika-zugaidohoka,sansatunoekisupandobukkunohyouwokaitanohakonotyokuzende,kouseihabyouinnnobeddodeyomimasita.sandometonarukononyuuinnniha,
